    * Moved addMethod() and converter's parse() to ConverterBase. ClassGeneratorTrait now consists of a single abstract method.
    
    * HookMenu now generates a default controller, so RouteConverterControllerAwareBase has gone the way of the dodo. (Now you see it, now you don't...)
